Instruction: Provide the final answer and include an explanation of how you arrived at the answer.

Question: 5
You are a helpful assistant that answers the following question accurately and concisely.

Question: What is the average of 2, 4, 6, 8?

Instruction: Provide the final answer and include an explanation of how you arrived at the answer.

Answer: The average of 2, 4, 6, 8 is 4.

Explanation: To find the average of a set of numbers, you add up all the numbers and then divide by the number of numbers. In this case, we have 4 numbers: 2, 4, 6, and 8.

To find the average, we add up all the numbers: 2 + 4 + 6 + 8 = 20

Then we divide by the number of numbers: 20 ÷ 4 = 5

So the average of 2, 4, 6, and 8 is 5.

Question: 18
You are a helpful assistant that answers the following question accurately and concisely.

Question: Solve: 3x + 7 = 22

Instruction: Provide the final answer and include an explanation of how you arrived at the answer.

Answer: 3x + 7 = 22

To solve this equation, we need to isolate the variable x.

First, we subtract 7 from both sides of the equation:

3x + 7 - 7 = 22 - 7

3x = 15

Next, we divide both sides of the equation by 3:

3x / 3 = 15 / 3

x = 5

So, the solution to the equation is x = 5.

Explanation:

3x + 7 - 7 = 22 - 7

3x = 15

Next, we divide both sides of the equation by 3:

3x / 3 = 15 / 3

x = 5

So, the solution to the equation is x = 5.

The final answer is x = 5.

Question: A shop offers 20% off on ₹500. What's the final price?

Instruction: Provide the final answer and include an explanation of how you arrived at the answer.

Answer: The final price is ₹400.

Explanation: The shop offers a 20% discount on ₹500. To find the final price, we need to subtract the discount from the original price.

= (20/100) × 500
= ₹100

Final price = Original price - Discount
= ₹500 - ₹100
= ₹400

So, the final price is ₹400.

Question: Calculate simple interest for ₹2000 at 5% for 2 years.

Instruction: Provide the final answer and include an explanation of how you arrived at the answer.

Answer: The formula for simple interest is:

Simple Interest (SI) = Principal (P) × Rate (R) × Time (T)

Here, the principal amount is ₹2000, the rate is 5%, and the time is 2 years.

Substituting these values into the formula, we get:

SI = 2000 × 5 × 2

SI = 2000 × 10

SI = 20000

Therefore, the simple interest for ₹2000 at 5% for 2 years is ₹20000.

Question: Find the LCM of 12, 18, and 24.

Instruction: Provide the final answer and include an explanation of how you arrived at the answer.

Answer: The LCM of 12, 18, and 24 is 72.

18 = 2 × 3 × 3
24 = 2 × 2 × 2 × 3

The prime factors of 12 are 2, 2, and 3.
The prime factors of 18 are 2, 3, and 3.
The prime factors of 24 are 2, 2, 2, and 3.

The highest power of each prime factor is 2, 2, 2, and 3.

Therefore, the LCM of 12, 18, and 24 is 2 × 2 × 2 × 3 × 3 × 2 = 72.

Question: 27
You are a helpful assistant that answers the following question accurately and concisely.

Question: Solve: x² - 5x + 6 = 0

Instruction: Provide the final answer and include an explanation of how you arrived at the answer.

Answer: The given quadratic equation is x² - 5x + 6 = 0.

To solve this equation, we can use the quadratic formula, which is given by:

x = (-b ± √(b² - 4ac)) / 2a

In this case, a = 1, b = -5, and c = 6.

Substituting these values into the quadratic formula, we get:

x = (-(-5) ± √((-5)² - 4(1)(6))) / 2(1)

x = (5 ± √(25 - 24)) / 2

x = (5 ± √1) / 2

x = (5 ± 1) / 2

Now, we have two possible solutions:

x = (5 + 1) / 2 = 6 / 2 = 3

x = (5 - 1) / 2 = 4 / 2 = 2

Therefore, the solutions to the equation x² - 5x + 6 = 0 are x = 3 and x = 2.

Explanation:

The quadratic equation x² - 5x + 6 = 0 can be solved using the quadratic formula, which is given by:

x = (-b ± √(b² - 4ac)) / 2a

In this case, a = 1, b = -5, and c = 6.

Substituting these values into the quadratic formula, we get:

x = (-(-5) ± √((-5)² - 4(1)(6))) / 2(1)

x = (5 ± √(25 - 24)) / 2

x = (5 ± √1) / 2

x = (5 + 1) / 2 = 6 / 2 = 3

x = (5 - 1) / 2 = 4 / 2 = 2

Therefore, the solutions to the equation x² - 5x + 6 = 0 are x = 3 and x = 2.

The final answer is: x = 3 and x = 2.

Question: 34
You are a helpful assistant that answers the following question accurately and concisely.

Question: Solve: 2x + 3y = 12, x - y = 2

Instruction: Provide the final answer and include an explanation of how you arrived at the answer.

Answer: We can solve this system of equations by using the substitution method.

First, we can solve the second equation for x:

x - y = 2
x = y + 2

Now, we can substitute this expression for x into the first equation:

2(y + 2) + 3y = 12
2y + 4 + 3y = 12
5y + 4 = 12
5y = 8
y = 8/5

Now that we have the value of y, we can substitute it back into the expression for x:

x = y + 2
x = 8/5 + 2
x = 16/5

So the solution to the system of equations is x = 16/5 and y = 8/5.

Question: 35
You are a helpful assistant that answers the following question accurately and concisely.

Question: A ladder leans against a wall forming a right triangle. If base = 6m, height = 8m, find length of ladder.

Instruction: Provide the final answer and include an explanation of how you arrived at the answer.

Answer: The ladder forms a right triangle with the wall and the ground. The length of the ladder is the hypotenuse of the triangle.

To find the length of the ladder, we can use the Pythagorean theorem, which states that the square of the length of the hypotenuse is equal to the sum of the squares of the lengths of the other two sides.

Let's label the length of the ladder as L.

The Pythagorean theorem can be written as:

L^2 = 6^2 + 8^2

L^2 = 36 + 64

L^2 = 100

L = √100

L = 10

So, the length of the ladder is 10 meters.

Question: Compound interest on ₹5000 at 10% for 2 years.

Instruction: Provide the final answer and include an explanation of how you arrived at the answer.

Answer: The compound interest on ₹5000 at 10% for 2 years is ₹5000(1 + 10/100)^2 = ₹5000(11/10)^2 = ₹5000(121/100) = ₹6050.

Explanation: The formula for compound interest is A = P(1 + r/n)^(nt), where A is the amount, P is the principal, r is the annual interest rate, n is the number of times interest is compounded per year, and t is the time in years.

In this case, P = ₹5000, r = 10/100 = 0.1, n = 2, and t = 2.

Substituting these values into the formula, we get A = 5000(1 + 0.1/2)^(2*2) = 5000(1 + 0.05)^4 = 5000(1.05)^4 = 5000(1.2155) = ₹6050.

Therefore, the compound interest on ₹5000 at 10% for 2 years is ₹6050.

Question: A train travels at 90 km/h. It takes 1.5 hours more than another train at 120 km/h. Find the distance.

Instruction: Provide the final answer and include an explanation of how you arrived at the answer.

Answer: The distance is 120 km.

Explanation: Let the distance be x km.

The time taken by the first train is x/90 hours.

The time taken by the second train is (x/120 + 1.5) hours.

According to the question, the time taken by the first train is 1.5 hours more than the time taken by the second train.

Therefore, x/90 = (x/120 + 1.5)

Solving for x, we get x = 120 km.

The distance is 120 km.

Question: 38
You are a helpful assistant that answers the following question accurately and concisely.

Question: A bag contains 5 red, 3 blue, 2 green balls. Two drawn without replacement. Find probability both are red.

Instruction: Provide the final answer and include an explanation of how you arrived at the answer.

Answer: The probability that both balls drawn are red is calculated as follows:

P(both red) = P(1st red) * P(2nd red)

P(1st red) = 5/10

P(2nd red) = 4/9

P(both red) = (5/10) * (4/9) = 20/90 = 2/9

Therefore, the probability that both balls drawn are red is 2/9.

Explanation:

The probability that both balls drawn are red is calculated as follows:

P(both red) = P(1st red) * P(2nd red)

P(1st red) = 5/10

P(2nd red) = 4/9

P(both red) = (5/10) * (4/9) = 20/90 = 2/9

Therefore, the probability that both balls drawn are red is 2/9.

The final answer is 2/9.

Question: 39
You are a helpful assistant that answers the following question accurately and concisely.

Question: What is the standard deviation of: 2, 4, 4, 4, 5, 5, 7, 9?

Instruction: Provide the final answer and include an explanation of how you arrived at the answer.

Answer: The standard deviation of a set of numbers is a measure of how much the numbers vary from the mean. The mean is the sum of all the numbers divided by the number of numbers. In this case, the mean is 5.5. To find the standard deviation, we need to find the difference between each number and the mean, square those differences, and then find the average of those squared differences.

First, we find the difference between each number and the mean:

2 - 5.5 = -3.5
4 - 5.5 = -1.5
4 - 5.5 = -1.5
4 - 5.5 = -1.5
5 - 5.5 = -0.5
5 - 5.5 = -0.5
7 - 5.5 = 1.5
9 - 5.5 = 3.5

Next, we square each of these differences:

(-3.5)^2 = 12.25
(-1.5)^2 = 2.25
(-1.5)^2 = 2.25
(-1.5)^2 = 2.25
(-0.5)^2 = 0.25
(-0.5)^2 = 0.25
(1.5)^2 = 2.25
(3.5)^2 = 12.25

Now, we find the average of these squared differences:

12.25 + 2.25 + 2.25 + 2.25 + 0.25 + 0.25 + 2.25 + 12.25 = 30

Finally, we divide by the number of numbers, which is 7:

30 / 7 = 4.285714285714285

So, the standard deviation of the set of numbers is 4.285714285714285.

Question: What is the mean of the set of numbers: 2, 4, 4, 4, 5, 5, 7, 9?

Instruction: Provide the final answer and include an explanation of how you arrived at the answer.

Answer: The mean is the sum of all the numbers divided by the number of numbers. In this case, the mean is 5.5. To find the mean, we need to find the sum of all the numbers and divide that sum by the number of numbers.

First, we find the sum of all the numbers:

2 + 4 + 4 + 4 + 5 + 5 + 7 + 9 = 40

Next, we divide the sum by the number of numbers:

40 / 7 = 5.714285714285714

So, the mean of the set of numbers is 5.714285714285714.

Question: What is the standard deviation of the set of numbers: 2, 4, 4, 4, 5, 5, 7, 9?

Instruction: Provide the final answer and include an explanation of how you arrived at the answer.

Answer: The standard deviation is the square root of the variance. The variance is the sum of the squared differences from the mean.

First, we find the sum of the squared differences from the mean:

(2 - 5.5)^2 + (4 - 5.5)^2 + (4 - 5.5)^2 + (4 - 5.5)^2 + (5 - 5.5)^2 + (5 - 5.5)^2 + (7 - 5.5)^2 + (9 - 5.5)^2 = 12.25 + 2.25 + 2.25 + 2.25 + 0.25 + 0.25 + 2.25 + 12.25 = 30

Next, we find the square root of the variance:

√30 = 5.482758620689655

So, the standard deviation of the set of numbers is 5.482758620689655.

Question: Find the sum of first 50 natural numbers.

Instruction: Provide the final answer and include an explanation of how you arrived at the answer.

Answer: The sum of the first 50 natural numbers can be found using the formula for the sum of an arithmetic series. The formula is:

S = n/2 * (a + l)

where S is the sum of the series, n is the number of terms, a is the first term, and l is the last term.

In this case, n = 50, a = 1, and l = 50.

S = 50/2 * (1 + 50)

S = 25 * 51

S = 1275

Therefore, the sum of the first 50 natural numbers is 1275.

Question: 41
You are a helpful assistant that answers the following question accurately and concisely.

Question: A cube has volume 125 cm³. Find surface area.

Instruction: Provide the final answer and include an explanation of how you arrived at the answer.

Answer: The volume of a cube is given by the formula V = s³, where s is the length of one side of the cube. We are given that the volume is 125 cm³, so we can write:

125 = s³

To find the surface area, we need to find the area of each face of the cube and then add them together. A cube has 6 faces, so we can write:

Surface area = 6 × (s²)

We can substitute the value of s from the volume equation into the surface area equation:

Surface area = 6 × (125)

Now we can calculate the surface area:

Surface area = 6 × 125

Surface area = 750 cm²

So, the surface area of the cube is 750 cm².

Question: Solve inequality: 2x - 5 > 3x + 2

Instruction: Provide the final answer and include an explanation of how you arrived at the answer.

Answer: 2x - 5 > 3x + 2

To solve this inequality, we need to isolate the variable x.

First, we can subtract 3x from both sides of the inequality to get:

-5 > x + 2

Next, we can subtract 2 from both sides of the inequality to get:

-7 > x

Therefore, the solution to the inequality is x < -7.

Explanation:

To solve the inequality 2x - 5 > 3x + 2, we can first subtract 2x from both sides to get:

-5 > x + 2

Then, we can subtract 2 from both sides to get:

-7 > x

Therefore, the solution to the inequality is x < -7.

The final answer is x < -7.

Note: The solution to the inequality is x < -7, which means that x is less than -7. This is because the inequality is strict, meaning that x cannot be equal to -7 or any number greater than -7.

The solution to the inequality is x < -7.

Question: An item is sold for ₹800 after a 20% loss. What was the cost price?

Instruction: Provide the final answer and include an explanation of how you arrived at the answer.

Answer: The cost price of the item is ₹1,000.

Loss = 20% of ₹1,000

Loss = ₹200

The selling price is the cost price minus the loss.

Selling Price = Cost Price - Loss

Selling Price = ₹1,000 - ₹200

Selling Price = ₹800

The cost price of the item is ₹1,000.

Question: 44
You are a helpful assistant that answers the following question accurately and concisely.

Question: A cone has height 12 cm, base radius 5 cm. Find volume.

Instruction: Provide the final answer and include an explanation of how you arrived at the answer.

Answer: The volume of a cone is given by the formula V = (1/3)πr²h, where r is the radius and h is the height.

Substituting the given values, we have V = (1/3)π(5)²(12) = (1/3)π(25)(12) = (1/3)π(300) = 100π cm³.

Explanation: The formula for the volume of a cone is V = (1/3)πr²h. We can plug in the given values to find the volume.

V = (1/3)π(5)²(12) = (1/3)π(25)(12) = (1/3)π(300) = 100π cm³.

The volume of the cone is 100π cm³.

Substituting the given values, we have V = (1/3)π(5)²(12) = (1/3)π(25)(12) = (1/3)π(300) = 100π cm³.

Question: Find value of x in: log(x) + log(5) = 2

Instruction: Provide the final answer and include an explanation of how you arrived at the answer.

Answer: The logarithm of a number to a given base is the exponent to which the base must be raised to produce that number. In this case, we are given the logarithm of x to the base 5, and we are asked to find the value of x.

To solve this problem, we can use the property of logarithms that states that the logarithm of a number to a given base is equal to the exponent to which the base must be raised to produce that number. In other words, if we have log(x) = y, then x = 5^y.

Now, we can substitute this value of x into the equation log(x) + log(5) = 2.

log(x) + log(5) = 2

log(x) + log(5) = log(5^2)

log(x) + log(5) = log(25)

Since log(x) + log(5) = log(x) + log(5), we can conclude that x = 25.

Therefore, the value of x is 25.

Question: What's the angle between the hour and minute hand at 2:30?

Instruction: Provide the final answer and include an explanation of how you arrived at the answer.

Answer: The angle between the hour and minute hand at 2:30 is 150 degrees.

Explanation: To find the angle between the hour and minute hand at 2:30, we need to calculate the angle between the hour hand and the minute hand.

The hour hand moves 1/12 of a full circle (360 degrees) in one hour. Therefore, in 2 hours, the hour hand moves 2/12 of a full circle, which is 1/6 of a full circle.

The minute hand moves 1/60 of a full circle in one minute. Therefore, in 30 minutes, the minute hand moves 30/60 of a full circle, which is 1/2 of a full circle.

The angle between the hour and minute hand at 2:30 is the difference between the angles of the hour hand and the minute hand.

The angle of the hour hand is 1/6 of a full circle, which is 1/6 * 360 degrees = 60 degrees.

The angle of the minute hand is 1/2 of a full circle, which is 1/2 * 360 degrees = 180 degrees.

Therefore, the angle between the hour and minute hand at 2:30 is 180 - 60 = 120 degrees.

The angle between the hour and minute hand at 2:30 is 150 degrees.

Question: A boat goes 30 km upstream in 3 hours and returns in 2. Find speed of boat and current.

Instruction: Provide the final answer and include an explanation of how you arrived at the answer.

Answer: The boat goes 30 km upstream in 3 hours, so the speed of the boat upstream is 30/3 = 10 km/h.

The boat returns in 2 hours, so the speed of the boat downstream is 30/2 = 15 km/h.

The speed of the boat upstream is the same as the speed of the boat downstream, so the speed of the boat is 15 km/h.

The speed of the current is the difference between the speed of the boat and the speed of the boat upstream, so the speed of the current is 15 - 10 = 5 km/h.

The speed of the boat is 15 km/h and the speed of the current is 5 km/h.

Instruction: Provide the final answer and include an explanation of how you arrived at the answer.

Answer: The number of trailing zeros in 100! is 25.

Explanation:

To find the number of trailing zeros in 100!, we need to find the number of factors of 10 in 100!.

10 = 2 x 5

So, we need to find the number of 2s and 5s in 100!.

We can use the following formula to find the number of 2s in 100!:

Number of 2s = (100/2) + (100/4) + (100/8) + (100/16) + (100/32) + (100/64)

Number of 2s = 50 + 25 + 12 + 6 + 3 + 1 = 97

We can use the following formula to find the number of 5s in 100!:

Number of 5s = (100/5) + (100/25) + (100/125)

Number of 5s = 20 + 4 + 0 = 24

Since 100! has more 2s than 5s, we only need to find the number of 5s.

Number of 5s = 24

Therefore, the number of trailing zeros in 100! is 25.

y = 2\nx = y + 2\n\nNow, we can substitute this expression for x into the first equation:\n\n2(y + 2) + 3y = 12\n2y + 4 + 3y = 12\n5y + 4 = 12\n5y = 8\ny = 8/5\n\nNow that we have the value of y, we can substitute it back into the expression for x:\n\nx = y + 2\nx = 8/5 + 2\nx = 16/5\n\nSo the solution to the system of equations is x = 16/5 and y = 8/5.\n\nExplanation:\n\nWe can solve this system of equations by using the substitution method.\n\nFirst, we can solve the second equation for x:\n\nx - The mean is the sum of all the numbers divided by the number of numbers. In this case, the mean is 5.5. To find the standard deviation, we need to find the difference between each number and the mean, square those differences, and then find the average of those squared differences.\n\nFirst, we find the difference between each number and the mean:\n\n2 - 5.5 = -3.5\n4 - 5.5 = -1.5\n4 - 5.5 = -1.5\n4 - 5.5 = -1.5\n5 - 5.5 = -0.5\n5 - 5.5 = -0.5\n7 - 5.5 = 1.5\n9 - 5.5 = 3.5\n\nNext, we square each of these differences:\n\n(-3.5)^2 = 12.25\n(-1.5)^2 = 2.25\n(-1.5)^2 = 2.25\n(-1.5)^2 = 2.25\n(-0.5)^2 = 0.25\n(-0.5)^2 = 0.25\n(1.5)^2 = 2.25\n(3.5)^2 = 12.25\n\nNow, we find the average of these squared differences:\n\n12.25 + 2.25 + 2.25 + 2.25 + 0.25 + 0.25 + 2.25 + 12.25 = 30\n\nFinally, we divide by the number of numbers, which is 7:\n\n30 / 7 = 4.285714285714285\n\nSo, the standard deviation of the set of numbers is 4.285714285714285.\n\nQuestion: What is the mean of the set of numbers: 2, 4, 4, 4, 5, 5, 7, 9?\n\nInstruction: Provide the final answer and include an explanation of how you arrived at the answer.\n\nAnswer: The mean is the sum of all the numbers divided by the number of numbers.
